   144	
   145	/**
   146	 * Trigger content for CustomSelect — 三種顯示模式分支(searchable+open / text / tag)
   147	 * 抽出降低 `CustomSelect` forwardRef body 長度;邏輯本質是純展示分流,無 hook / ref。
   148	 */
   149	function CustomSelectTriggerContent({
   150	  searchable,
   151	  open,
   152	  isTextDisplay,
   153	  size,
   154	  value,
   155	  selectedLabel,
   156	  selectedOpt,
   157	  SelectedIcon,
   158	  StartIcon,
   159	  iconSize,
   160	  placeholder,
   161	  search,
   162	  setSearch,
   163	  inputRef,
   164	  selectedItemRenderer,
   165	}: {
   166	  searchable: boolean
   167	  open: boolean
   168	  isTextDisplay: boolean
   169	  size: 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg'
   170	  value?: string | null
   171	  selectedLabel: string
   172	  selectedOpt?: SelectOption
   173	  SelectedIcon?: LucideIcon
   174	  StartIcon?: LucideIcon
   175	  iconSize: number
   176	  placeholder?: string
   177	  search: string
   178	  setSearch: (v: string) => void
   179	  inputRef: React.RefObject<HTMLInputElement | null>
   180	  selectedItemRenderer?: (selectedOpt: SelectOption) => React.ReactNode
   181	}): React.ReactNode {
   182	  // Searchable + open: 顯示搜尋 input
   183	  // 2026-05-15 Bug 2 fix(Claude+Codex Step 5 比稿 consensus,user verbatim「就 A」):
   184	  // 撤掉 native `<input placeholder=selectedLabel>` 不可靠 ellipsis renderer(browser-specific
   185	  // placeholder painting,user 抓「placeholder 直接被截掉沒 ellipsis」)。改 span overlay:
   186	  // - input native placeholder 限「搜尋…」/「請選擇人員」trigger empty hint(無 selectedLabel)
   187	  // - sibling `<span aria-hidden pointer-events-none absolute inset-0 truncate>` 在 search='' 且
   188	  //   有 selectedLabel 時 overlay 顯該人名(memory aid,truncate-with-ellipsis 可控)
   189	  // 對齊 spec.md §B row 4「open + inline-search + 選 1 人 → input cursor + placeholder = 該人名 + ellipsis」。
   190	  // a11y guard(per codex Q2 reply):input aria-label / accessible name 來自 field/label/aria-label,
   191	  // **不**依賴 placeholder 當 label;overlay span aria-hidden + pointer-events-none。
   192	  if (searchable && open) {
   193	    const triggerEmptyPlaceholder = placeholder || '搜尋…' // i18n-allow: DS fallback
   194	    const showSelectedOverlay = !search && selectedLabel
   195	    return (
   196	      <span className="relative flex-1 min-w-0 inline-flex items-center">
   197	        {StartIcon && <ItemPrefix><StartIcon size={iconSize} className="text-fg-muted pointer-events-none" aria-hidden /></ItemPrefix>}
   198	        <input
   199	          ref={inputRef as React.RefObject<HTMLInputElement>}
   200	          value={search}
   201	          onChange={(e) => setSearch(e.target.value)}
   202	          // Native placeholder 限 trigger empty hint(無 selectedLabel 時);若已 selected,留空交給 overlay span
   203	          placeholder={showSelectedOverlay ? '' : triggerEmptyPlaceholder}
   204	          className={cn(bareInputStyles, 'cursor-text')}
   205	          autoFocus
   206	        />
   207	        {showSelectedOverlay && (
   208	          <span
   209	            aria-hidden="true"
   210	            className="pointer-events-none absolute inset-0 inline-flex items-center truncate text-fg-muted"
   211	            // 用 inset-0 + items-center 跟 input baseline 對齊;truncate 提供可控 ellipsis(不像 native placeholder)
   212	            // 注意 padding 由 input 內 set,overlay span 用相同 box-sizing 對齊
   213	          >
   214	            {selectedLabel}
   215	          </span>
   216	        )}
   217	      </span>
   218	    )
   219	  }
   220	  // **selectedItemRenderer slot**(2026-05-07 v15.5):consumer 客製 selected display(e.g.
   221	  // PeoplePicker 接 PersonDisplay)。優先於 isTextDisplay / Tag 預設 path,但 empty value
   222	  // 仍走 placeholder。對齊 PeoplePicker = Select wrapper SSOT。
   223	  if (selectedItemRenderer && value && selectedOpt) {
   224	    return (
   225	      <>
   226	        {StartIcon && <ItemPrefix><StartIcon size={iconSize} className="text-fg-muted pointer-events-none" aria-hidden /></ItemPrefix>}
   227	        {/* 2026-05-14 item-anatomy SSOT fix(per codex H2 propagation 斷點):加 nakedCellRowModeAlign
   228	            → autoRowHeight cell 內 selected renderer 也對齊 first-line,不再 vertical-center 整 row。 */}
   229	        <span className={cn("flex-1 min-w-0 inline-flex items-center", nakedCellRowModeAlign)}>{selectedItemRenderer(selectedOpt)}</span>
   230	      </>
   231	    )
   232	  }
   233	  // Text display: 純文字 + optional value icon
   234	  if (isTextDisplay) {
   235	    return (
   236	      <>
   237	        {StartIcon && <ItemPrefix><StartIcon size={iconSize} className="text-fg-muted pointer-events-none" aria-hidden /></ItemPrefix>}
   238	        {!StartIcon && SelectedIcon && value && <ItemPrefix><SelectedIcon size={iconSize} className="pointer-events-none" aria-hidden /></ItemPrefix>}
   239	        <span className={cn('flex-1 min-w-0 truncate', !value && 'text-fg-muted')}>
   240	          {value ? selectedLabel : (placeholder ?? '選擇…')}
   241	        </span>
   242	      </>
   243	    )
   244	  }
   245	  // Tag display: 用 option 的 tagVariant
   246	  return (
   247	    <>
   248	      {value && selectedOpt?.tagVariant
   249	        ? <Tag size={size} color={selectedOpt.tagVariant as 'blue' | 'green' | 'red' | 'yellow' | 'neutral'} className="shrink-0 pointer-events-none">{selectedLabel}</Tag>
   250	        : value
   251	          ? <Tag size={size} className="shrink-0 pointer-events-none">{selectedLabel}</Tag>
   252	          : <span className="text-fg-muted">{placeholder ?? '選擇…'}</span>
   253	      }
   254	      <span className="flex-1" />
   255	    </>
   256	  )
   257	}
   258	CustomSelectTriggerContent.displayName = 'CustomSelectTriggerContent'
   259	
   260	// ── Shared readonly/disabled/display render ─────────────────────────────────
   261	function ReadonlyDisplay({
   262	  mode, variant: variantProp, size, options, value, display, startIcon: StartIcon, className, placeholder, showDisplayEndIcon,
   263	}: Pick<SelectProps, 'mode' | 'variant' | 'size' | 'options' | 'value' | 'display' | 'startIcon' | 'className' | 'placeholder' | 'showDisplayEndIcon'>) {
   264	  const resolvedMode = mode ?? 'readonly'
   265	  const variant = variantProp ?? 'default'
   266	  const sz = size ?? 'md'
   267	  const iconSize = getIconSize(sz)
   268	  const label = options?.find(o => o.value === value)?.label ?? value
   269	  const iconColor = resolvedMode === 'disabled' ? 'text-fg-disabled' : 'text-fg-muted'
   270	  const isTextDisplay = display !== 'tag'
   271	  // K10+K14 fix(2026-05-04):disabled mode placeholder/empty 顯示色 → fg-disabled(neutral-6),非 fg-muted(neutral-7)
   272	  //   user canonical:disabled 顯著性優於 muted。同時 plain mode 必須 respect placeholder prop(之前忽略 = bug)
   273	  const emptyColorCls = resolvedMode === 'disabled' ? 'text-fg-disabled' : 'text-fg-muted'
   274	  const emptyText = placeholder ?? EMPTY_DISPLAY
   275	
   276	  // mode='display':2 path(2026-05-08 D path Phase 1 Select canary)
   277	  //   ❌ 預設(無 showDisplayEndIcon):純內容輸出 bare span/Tag(原行為,backward compat)
   278	  //      對齊原 SelectDisplay sub-component(retired)。readonly / disabled 仍走下方 fieldWrapperStyles。
   279	  //   ✅ showDisplayEndIcon=true(DataTable cell opt-in):Field naked-display wrapper +
   280	  //      ChevronDown ItemSuffix。SSOT canonical 跟 readonly/edit/disabled mode 同 DOM 結構。
   281	  //      Authority: data-table.spec.md:204 + inline-action.spec.md:157「Field family endAction」
   282	  if (resolvedMode === 'display') {
   283	    if (!showDisplayEndIcon) {
   284	      // 2026-05-14 I2 fix(spec contract (e) display typography canonical):bare span 必套
   285	      // `fieldDisplayTextClass(sz)`(sm/md→text-body,lg→text-body-lg)— 對齊跨 Field
   286	      // family display 視覺尺寸統一。
   287	      if (!value) return <span className={cn(fieldDisplayTextClass(sz), 'text-fg-muted', className)}>{emptyText}</span>
   288	      if (isTextDisplay) return <span className={cn(fieldDisplayTextClass(sz), 'truncate', className)}>{label}</span>
   289	      const selOpt = options?.find(o => o.value === value)
   290	      const tVariant = selOpt?.tagVariant as 'blue' | 'green' | 'red' | 'yellow' | 'neutral' | undefined
   291	      return <Tag size={sz} color={tVariant} className={className}>{label}</Tag>
   292	    }
   293	    // D path opt-in: Field naked-display wrapper + ItemSuffix ChevronDown
   294	    const selOpt = options?.find(o => o.value === value)
   295	    const tVariant = selOpt?.tagVariant as 'blue' | 'green' | 'red' | 'yellow' | 'neutral' | undefined
   296	    return (
   297	      <div
   298	        className={cn(fieldWrapperStyles({ mode: 'display', variant, size: sz }), value && !isTextDisplay && tagPadding[sz], className)}
   299	        data-field-mode="display"
   300	      >
   301	        {isTextDisplay ? (
   302	          <span className={cn(bareInputStyles, 'flex-1 min-w-0 truncate', !value && emptyColorCls)}>
   303	            {value ? label : emptyText}
   304	          </span>
   305	        ) : value ? (
   306	          <Tag size={sz} color={tVariant}>{label}</Tag>
   307	        ) : (
   308	          <span className={cn('flex-1 min-w-0', emptyColorCls)}>{emptyText}</span>
   309	        )}
   310	        <ItemSuffix><ChevronDown size={iconSize} className="text-fg-muted pointer-events-none" aria-hidden /></ItemSuffix>
   311	      </div>
   312	    )
   313	  }
   314	
   315	  if (isTextDisplay) {
   316	    return (
   317	      <div className={cn(fieldWrapperStyles({ mode: resolvedMode, variant, size: sz }), className)} data-field-mode={resolvedMode}>
   318	        {StartIcon && <ItemPrefix><StartIcon size={iconSize} className={cn('pointer-events-none', iconColor)} aria-hidden /></ItemPrefix>}
   319	        <span className={cn('flex-1 min-w-0 truncate', resolvedMode === 'disabled' && 'text-fg-disabled')}>
   320	          {value ? label : <span className={emptyColorCls}>{emptyText}</span>}
   321	        </span>
   322	      </div>
   323	    )
   324	  }
   325	
   326	  const selectedOpt = options?.find(o => o.value === value)
   327	  const tagVariant = selectedOpt?.tagVariant as 'blue' | 'green' | 'red' | 'yellow' | 'neutral' | undefined
   328	
   329	  return (
   330	    <div className={cn(fieldWrapperStyles({ mode: resolvedMode, variant, size: sz }), value && tagPadding[sz], className)} data-field-mode={resolvedMode}>
   331	      {value ? <Tag size={sz} color={tagVariant}>{label}</Tag> : <span className={emptyColorCls}>{emptyText}</span>}
   332	    </div>
   333	  )
   334	}
   335	
   336	// ── Native Select (mobile) ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   337	
   338	// code-quality-allow: long-function — foundational composite main body — 拆 sub-fn 會複雜化 local state / ref / context binding
   339	const NativeSelect = React.forwardRef<HTMLSelectElement, SelectProps>(
   340	  ({ mode = 'edit', variant: variantProp, error: errorProp = false, size = 'md', options, value, onChange, placeholder, className, disabled: disabledProp, clearable = false, display = 'plain', startIcon: StartIcon, showDisplayEndIcon, id: idProp, 'aria-describedby': ariaDescribedByProp, 'aria-errormessage': ariaErrorMessageProp, ...props }, ref) => {
   341	    const fieldCtx = useFieldContext()
   342	    const error = errorProp || (fieldCtx?.invalid ?? false)
   343	    const disabled = disabledProp ?? fieldCtx?.disabled
   344	    const resolvedMode = disabled ? 'disabled' : mode
   345	    const variant: FieldVariant = variantProp ?? fieldCtx?.variant ?? 'default'
   346	    const iconSize = getIconSize(size)
   347	    const showClear = clearable && value && resolvedMode === 'edit'
   348	    const isTextDisplay = display === 'plain'
   349	    const selectRef = React.useRef<HTMLSelectElement | null>(null)
   350	    const setSelectRef = React.useCallback((el: HTMLSelectElement | null) => {
   351	      selectRef.current = el
   352	      if (typeof ref === 'function') ref(el)
   353	      else if (ref) (ref as React.MutableRefObject<HTMLSelectElement | null>).current = el
   354	    }, [ref])
   355	
   356	    if (resolvedMode !== 'edit') {
   357	      return <ReadonlyDisplay mode={resolvedMode} variant={variant} size={size} options={options} value={value} display={display} startIcon={StartIcon} className={className} placeholder={placeholder} showDisplayEndIcon={showDisplayEndIcon} />
   358	    }
   359	
   360	    const selectEl = (
   361	      <select
   362	        ref={setSelectRef}
   363	        id={idProp ?? fieldCtx?.id}
   364	        value={value ?? ''}
   365	        onChange={onChange ? (e) => onChange(e.target.value) : undefined}
   366	        disabled={disabled}
   367	        aria-invalid={error || undefined}
   368	        aria-required={fieldCtx?.required || undefined}
   369	        aria-describedby={ariaDescribedByProp ?? fieldCtx?.descriptionId}
   370	        aria-errormessage={ariaErrorMessageProp ?? (error ? fieldCtx?.errorId : undefined)}
   371	        className={cn(bareInputStyles, 'cursor-pointer appearance-none', !value && 'text-fg-muted', !isTextDisplay && value && 'absolute inset-0 w-full h-full opacity-0 z-0')}
   372	        {...props}
   373	      >
   374	        {placeholder && <option value="" disabled>{placeholder}</option>}
   375	        {options.map(opt => <option key={opt.value} value={opt.value}>{opt.label}</option>)}
   376	      </select>
   377	    )
   378	
   379	    const clearEl = showClear ? (
   380	      <SelectClearButton size={size ?? 'md'} onClear={() => onChange?.('')} />
   381	    ) : null
   382	
   383	    const chevronEl = (
   384	      <ItemSuffix className="relative z-10 pointer-events-none">
   385	        <ChevronDown size={iconSize} className="text-fg-muted" aria-hidden />
   386	      </ItemSuffix>
   387	    )
   388	    const selectedOpt = options?.find(o => o.value === value)
   389	    const label = selectedOpt?.label ?? value
   390	    const nativeTagVariant = selectedOpt?.tagVariant as 'blue' | 'green' | 'red' | 'yellow' | 'neutral' | undefined
   391	    const SelectedOptIcon = selectedOpt?.icon
   392	
   393	    if (!isTextDisplay) {
   394	      return (
   395	        <div className={cn(fieldWrapperStyles({ mode: 'edit', variant: variant, size }), value && tagPadding[size], 'relative',
   396	          error && ['border-error hover:border-error-hover', 'focus-within:border-error focus-within:hover:border-error'], className)}
   397	          style={{ paddingRight: '0.75rem' }} data-field-mode="edit" data-error={error ? '' : undefined}>
   398	          {value ? <Tag size={size} color={nativeTagVariant} className="shrink-0 relative z-10 pointer-events-none">{label}</Tag> : <span className="text-fg-muted">{placeholder ?? '選擇...'}</span>}
   399	          {selectEl}
   400	          <span className="flex-1" />
   401	          {clearEl}
   402	          {chevronEl}
   403	        </div>
   404	      )
   405	    }
   406	
   407	    return (
   408	      <div className={cn(fieldWrapperStyles({ mode: 'edit', variant: variant, size }),
   409	        error && ['border-error hover:border-error-hover', 'focus-within:border-error focus-within:hover:border-error'], className)}
   410	        data-field-mode="edit" data-error={error ? '' : undefined}>
   411	        {StartIcon && <ItemPrefix><StartIcon size={iconSize} className="text-fg-muted pointer-events-none" aria-hidden /></ItemPrefix>}
   412	        {!StartIcon && SelectedOptIcon && value && <ItemPrefix><SelectedOptIcon size={iconSize} className="pointer-events-none" aria-hidden /></ItemPrefix>}
   413	        {selectEl}
   414	        {clearEl}
   415	        {chevronEl}
   416	      </div>
   417	    )
   418	  }
   419	)
   420	NativeSelect.displayName = 'NativeSelect'
   421	
   422	// ── Custom Select (desktop — consumes SelectMenu) ────────────────────────
   423	
   424	// code-quality-allow: long-function — foundational composite main body — 拆 sub-fn 會複雜化 local state / ref / context binding
   425	const CustomSelect = React.forwardRef<HTMLDivElement, SelectProps>(
   426	  ({ mode = 'edit', variant: variantProp, error: errorProp = false, size = 'md', options, groups, value, onChange, placeholder, className, disabled: disabledProp, clearable = false, display = 'plain', startIcon: StartIcon, searchable = false, loading, minRows, defaultOpen = false, onOpenChange, selectedItemRenderer, showDisplayEndIcon, id: idProp, 'aria-describedby': ariaDescribedByProp, 'aria-errormessage': ariaErrorMessageProp, 'aria-label': ariaLabel }, ref) => {
   427	    const fieldCtx = useFieldContext()
   428	    const error = errorProp || (fieldCtx?.invalid ?? false)
   429	    const disabled = disabledProp ?? fieldCtx?.disabled
   430	    const resolvedMode = disabled ? 'disabled' : mode
   431	    const variant: FieldVariant = variantProp ?? fieldCtx?.variant ?? 'default'
   432	    const iconSize = getIconSize(size)
   433	    const showClear = clearable && value && resolvedMode === 'edit'
   434	    const isTextDisplay = display === 'plain'
   435	
   436	    const [open, setOpen] = React.useState(defaultOpen)
   437	    const [search, setSearch] = React.useState('')
   438	    const inputRef = React.useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null)
   439	
   440	    // 關閉時清搜尋
   441	    React.useEffect(() => { if (!open) setSearch('') }, [open])
   442	
   443	    // **React #310 fix(2026-05-04)**:所有 hooks 必在任何 early return 前 call,
   444	    //   否則 disabled→edit 切換時 hook count 變動 → React 死亡。
   445	    //   原本 useMemo(L280, L291) 在 early return 之後 = latent bug,K13 觸發(filter Op 從 disabled
   446	    //   變 edit 當 user 選欄位)。修法:把所有 useMemo 提到 early return 之前。
   447	    const selectedOpt = options?.find(o => o.value === value)
   448	    // 2026-05-06 v9.1:value 不在 options 也要顯示原值(不沉默丟失)。原 fallback `''` 致
   449	    // SelectCell 開 edit 時若 cell value 不在當前 options(e.g. 上游資料漂移 / options async
   450	    // 後到 / 跨 dataset),trigger 顯示空白 — user 報「value 不見」。對齊 ReadonlyDisplay 同
   451	    // 級 fallback `?? value`。
   452	    const selectedLabel = selectedOpt?.label ?? value ?? ''
   453	    const SelectedIcon = selectedOpt?.icon
   454	    // ── 過濾選項 ──
   455	    const filteredOptions = searchable && search
   456	      ? options.filter(o => o.label.toLowerCase().includes(search.toLowerCase()))
   457	      : options
   458	    // ── 轉換 SelectOption → SelectMenuOption(必在 early return 前) ──
   459	    // Issue 4(2026-05-10):forward avatar / description / disabled SSOT(per SelectMenuOption schema)。
   460	    const menuOptions: SelectMenuOption[] = React.useMemo(
   461	      () => filteredOptions.map(opt => ({
   462	        value: opt.value,
   463	        label: opt.label,
   464	        icon: isTextDisplay ? opt.icon : undefined,
   465	        avatar: opt.avatar,
   466	        description: opt.description,
   467	        disabled: opt.disabled,
   468	        group: opt.group,
   469	      })),
   470	      [filteredOptions, isTextDisplay]
   471	    )
   472	    // ── Tag display 自訂 label 渲染(必在 early return 前) ──
   473	    const renderLabel = React.useMemo(() => {
   474	      if (isTextDisplay) return undefined
   475	      return (menuOpt: SelectMenuOption) => {
   476	        const srcOpt = options.find(o => o.value === menuOpt.value)
   477	        if (srcOpt?.tagVariant) {
   478	          return <Tag size={size} color={srcOpt.tagVariant as 'blue' | 'green' | 'red' | 'yellow' | 'neutral'}>{menuOpt.label}</Tag>
   479	        }
   480	        return menuOpt.label
   481	      }
   482	    }, [isTextDisplay, options, size])
   483	
   484	    // **React #310 fix v2(2026-05-04)**:`handleValueChange` useCallback 也必在 early return 前
   485	    //   原本 L306(early return 後)→ disabled→edit 切換時 hook count 仍變 → #310 持續
   486	    const handleValueChange = React.useCallback(
   487	      (newValue: string | string[]) => {
   488	        const v = Array.isArray(newValue) ? newValue[0] : newValue
   489	        onChange?.(v)
   490	      },
   491	      [onChange]
   492	    )
   493	
   494	    // Early return AFTER all hooks(disabled / readonly / display mode 走 ReadonlyDisplay)
   495	    if (resolvedMode !== 'edit') {
   496	      return <ReadonlyDisplay mode={resolvedMode} variant={variant} size={size} options={options} value={value} display={display} startIcon={StartIcon} className={className} placeholder={placeholder} showDisplayEndIcon={showDisplayEndIcon} />
   497	    }
   498	
   499	    const clearEl = showClear ? (
   500	      <SelectClearButton size={size ?? 'md'} onClear={() => onChange?.('')} stopPropagation />
   501	    ) : null
   502	
   503	    const chevronEl = (
   504	      <ItemSuffix>
   505	        <ChevronDown size={iconSize} className={cn('text-fg-muted transition-transform', open && 'rotate-180')} aria-hidden />
   506	      </ItemSuffix>
   507	    )
   508	
   509	    const triggerContent = (
   510	      <CustomSelectTriggerContent
   511	        searchable={searchable}
   512	        open={open}
   513	        isTextDisplay={isTextDisplay}
   514	        size={size}
   515	        value={value}
   516	        selectedLabel={selectedLabel}
   517	        selectedOpt={selectedOpt}
   518	        SelectedIcon={SelectedIcon}
   519	        StartIcon={StartIcon}
   520	        iconSize={iconSize}
   521	        placeholder={placeholder}
   522	        search={search}
   523	        setSearch={setSearch}
   524	        inputRef={inputRef}
   525	        selectedItemRenderer={selectedItemRenderer}
   526	      />
   527	    )
   528	
   529	    // hooks(filteredOptions / menuOptions / renderLabel / handleValueChange)已全 hoist(React #310 fix v2)
   530	
   531	    const trigger = (
   532	      <div
   533	        ref={ref}
   534	        id={idProp ?? fieldCtx?.id}
   535	        role="combobox"
   536	        aria-expanded={open}
   537	        aria-haspopup="listbox"
   538	        aria-label={ariaLabel}
   539	        aria-invalid={error || undefined}
   540	        aria-required={fieldCtx?.required || undefined}
   541	        aria-describedby={ariaDescribedByProp ?? fieldCtx?.descriptionId}
   542	        aria-errormessage={ariaErrorMessageProp ?? (error ? fieldCtx?.errorId : undefined)}
   543	        tabIndex={0}
   544	        className={cn(
   545	          fieldWrapperStyles({ mode: 'edit', variant: variant, size }),
   546	          !isTextDisplay && value && !searchable && tagPadding[size],
   547	          // 2026-05-06 v13.3 SSOT retire:per-control `open && 'border-primary'` 移除。Field default
   548	          // state machine `data-[state=open]:border-border-hover`(灰深)處理 open;若 trigger focused
   549	          // (Radix focus on open),focus-within:!border-primary 強制勝出顯藍。focus dominates everything
   550	          // 全 DS 一致(Material/Polaris/Ant 共識),改 Field default 一處全 control 自動跟動。
   551	          error && ['border-error hover:border-error-hover', 'focus-within:border-error focus-within:hover:border-error'],
   552	          'cursor-pointer',
   553	          className,
   554	        )}
   555	        style={!isTextDisplay ? { paddingRight: '0.75rem' } : undefined}
   556	        data-field-mode="edit"
   557	        data-error={error ? '' : undefined}
   558	        onKeyDown={(e) => {
   559	          if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
   560	            if (!searchable) { e.preventDefault(); setOpen(true) }
   561	          }
   562	          if (e.key === 'Escape') setOpen(false)
   563	        }}
   564	      >
   565	        {triggerContent}
   566	        {clearEl}
   567	        {chevronEl}
   568	      </div>
   569	    )
   570	
   571	    return (
   572	      <SelectMenu
   573	        options={menuOptions}
   574	        groups={groups}
   575	        value={value ?? null}
   576	        onValueChange={handleValueChange}
   577	        searchable={false}
   578	        loading={loading}
   579	        size={size}
   580	        minRows={minRows}
   581	        open={open}
   582	        onOpenChange={(o) => { setOpen(o); onOpenChange?.(o) }}
   583	        renderLabel={renderLabel}
   584	        onOpenAutoFocus={searchable ? (e) => { e.preventDefault(); inputRef.current?.focus() } : undefined}
   585	      >
   586	        {trigger}
   587	      </SelectMenu>
   588	    )
   589	  }
   590	)
   591	CustomSelect.displayName = 'CustomSelect'
   592	
   593	// ── Public component（自動偵測 mobile / desktop）──────────────────────────────
   594	
   595	const Select = React.forwardRef<HTMLSelectElement | HTMLDivElement, SelectProps>(
   596	  (props, ref) => {
   597	    const isMobile = useIsTouchDevice()
   598	
   599	    if (isMobile) {
   600	      return <NativeSelect ref={ref as React.Ref<HTMLSelectElement>} {...props} />
   601	    }
   602	
   603	    return <CustomSelect ref={ref as React.Ref<HTMLDivElement>} {...props} />
   604	  }
   605	)
   606	Select.displayName = 'Select'
   607	
   608	// Story auto-compile metadata — Phase 1 mechanical migration(2026-04-24)
   609	// Phase 2 fill needed: purpose descriptions + when rationale + world-class refs
   610	export const selectMeta = {
   611	  component: 'Select',
   612	  family: 4,
   613	  variants: {
   614	
   615	  },
   616	  sizes: {
   617	
   618	  },
   619	  states: ['default', 'hover', 'active', 'focus-visible', 'disabled'],
   620	  tokens: {
   621	    bg: [],
   622	    fg: ['text-fg-disabled', 'text-fg-muted'],
   623	    ring: [],
   624	  },
   625	} as const
   626	
   627	export { Select }

    10	import { ItemPrefix } from '@/design-system/patterns/element-anatomy/item-anatomy'
    11	import {
    12	  getAvatarStackVisibleCount,

    17	// ── Types ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    18	
    19	// PersonData 承載 NameCard 所需的完整資訊。DS 全域 person avatar 的 hoverCard NameCard 永遠
    20	// 顯示同一組 sections(name + subtitle + status + 4 default fields + 自訂 fields + actions + View more)
    21	// — 缺資料顯 placeholder,不會 collapse。對齊 avatar.spec.md「person avatar hover → NameCard」
    22	// DS-wide canonical(2026-05-06 v11 always-render schema 升級)。
    23	export interface PersonData {
    24	  name: string
    25	  avatarUrl?: string
    26	  /** 角色 / 部門 / ID 等 meta 單行(NameCard subtitle) */
    27	  description?: string
    28	  /** Presence 狀態(對齊 Avatar presence canonical)。**2026-05-14 v12 update**(per user 拍板):
    29	   *  production 每 user 一定有 presence state,**undefined = loading transient(資料還沒讀到)**,
    30	   *  不是「user 沒設定」。NameCard 在 undefined 期間隱藏整 status block,**禁** render「Status not set」
    31	   *  placeholder 文字。 */
    32	  status?: 'online' | 'away' | 'busy' | 'offline'
    33	  /** Status 訊息(NameCard status section)。只在 status defined 時 render,缺則顯 `—` placeholder。
    34	   *  Status undefined 整 block skip(無 statusMessage 也跟著 skip)。 */
    35	  statusMessage?: React.ReactNode
    36	  /** **2026-05-07 v15.7 user directive**:NameCard default 只 render `id` + `employeeNumber`,
    37	   *  其他 description 一律 opt-in by consumer 透過 `fields` array prop。對齊
    38	   *  `NAMECARD_DEFAULT_FIELD_KEYS = ['id', 'employeeNumber']`。 */
    39	  id?: string
    40	  employeeNumber?: string
    41	  /** 自訂額外 fields(在 default fields 之後 append)。Email / Phone / Department / Location
    42	   *  / 任何其他 description 一律走這個 prop(opt-in,consumer 自選)。 */
    43	  fields?: { label: string; value: string }[]
    44	  /** 跳至完整 profile 頁的 handler(hover NameCard 必含,不傳時 fallback noop placeholder) */
    45	  onViewProfile?: () => void
    46	}
    47	
    48	export type PersonValue = string | PersonData
    49	
    50	function resolvePerson(value: PersonValue): PersonData {
    51	  return typeof value === 'string' ? { name: value } : value
    52	}
    53	
    54	// buildPersonNameCard — DS 全域 person avatar hoverCard 的 canonical NameCard JSX 建構器。
    55	// SSOT for「avatar hover NameCard 一致視覺」— 任何 person avatar consumer 都走這個 helper,
    56	// 不可繞道直接 build NameCard。
    57	//
    58	// **2026-05-07 v15.7 user directive**:default field values 只 `id` + `employeeNumber`,
    59	// 對齊 NAMECARD_DEFAULT_FIELD_KEYS。其他 description(email/phone/department/location/etc)
    60	// consumer 想顯式透過 `person.fields` opt-in 傳入。
    61	function buildPersonNameCard(person: PersonData): React.ReactNode {
    62	  return (
    63	    <NameCard
    64	      name={person.name}
    65	      subtitle={person.description}
    66	      avatar={{ src: person.avatarUrl, alt: person.name }}
    67	      status={person.status}
    68	      statusMessage={person.statusMessage}
    69	      defaultFieldValues={{
    70	        id: person.id,
    71	        employeeNumber: person.employeeNumber,
    72	      }}
    73	      fields={person.fields}
    74	      actions={<NameCardDefaultActions />}
    75	      // onViewMore hover context 必含(avatar.spec.md canonical)。consumer 傳
    76	      // `onViewProfile` 則用真 handler,否則 noop placeholder(UI 仍渲染 View more
    77	      // footer,避免 preview 變死路)。
    78	      onViewMore={person.onViewProfile ?? (() => {})}
    79	    />
    80	  )
    81	}
    82	
    83	// ── Avatar Size ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    84	// 與 Tag 高度對齊:sm=20px, md/lg=24px(對齊 item-anatomy AVATAR_SIZE.inline)
    85	
    86	const AVATAR_PX: Record<'sm' | 'md' | 'lg', number> = { sm: 20, md: 24, lg: 24 }
    87	
    88	// ── PersonAvatar ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    89	// Consume DS `Avatar` primitive(2026-04-22 refactor,M1 SSOT consumption)+ 預設 NameCard
    90	// hoverCard(avatar.spec.md DS-wide「person avatar hover → NameCard」canonical)。
    91	//
    92	// 之前用 local `<img>` / `<User icon />` hand-craft 繞過 DS Avatar,違反 M1。本次 refactor:
    93	// - 所有 person avatar 經過 DS Avatar primitive(size 對應 uiSize family,fallback / icon / badge 集中管理)
    94	// - 人員資訊 → NameCard(subtitle = description,actions = NameCardDefaultActions)
    95	
    96	// 2026-05-13 (a) perf fix(per codex Layer C HoverCard subtree dominant):
    97	// useMemo `buildPersonNameCard` per-person stable ref。原 every render call → new JSX ref →
    98	// Avatar.memo bails → HoverCard subtree 重建。Stable ref → memo skip → big win on scroll。
    99	//
   100	// (c) push-up scroll-defer:當 DataTable virtualizer.isScrolling=true,**完全不 build NameCard**
   101	// (Avatar 收 undefined → 跳 HoverCard wrapper)。原 (c) v1 在 Avatar 層 skip wrapper 但 NameCard
   102	// JSX subtree 仍在此處 build → 浪費 React reconciliation work。push 到此處才真省。
   103	function PersonAvatar({
   104	  person,
   105	  size = 'md',
   106	  className = '',
   107	  style,
   108	}: {
   109	  person: PersonData
   110	  size?: 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg'
   111	  className?: string
   112	  style?: React.CSSProperties
   113	}) {
   114	  const isTableScrolling = useTableIsScrolling()
   115	  const nameCard = React.useMemo(
   116	    () => (isTableScrolling ? undefined : buildPersonNameCard(person)),
   117	    [person, isTableScrolling]
   118	  )
   119	  return (
   120	    <Avatar
   121	      src={person.avatarUrl}
   122	      alt={person.name}
   123	      size={AVATAR_PX[size]}
   124	      className={className}
   125	      style={style}
   126	      hoverCard={nameCard}
   127	    />
   128	  )
   129	}
   130	
   131	// ── Single Person Display ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
   132	
   133	// 2026-05-14 item-anatomy SSOT fix(per codex+Layer A 共識 path (a) + user 拍板「全部做完」):
   134	// outer 改 items-start + Avatar 外包 ItemPrefix primitive consumption。單行視覺 = items-center 等效;
   135	// 多行(autoRowHeight cell)避免 avatar+name center 整 row 不對齊 first-line text top。M1 消費既有
   136	// 對齊 TreeView / MenuItem / SelectionItem 共用 ItemPrefix wrap chevron/icon/avatar canonical。
   137	function PersonDisplay({ value, size = 'md' }: { value?: PersonValue | null; size?: 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg' }) {
   138	  if (!value) return <span className="text-fg-muted">{EMPTY_DISPLAY}</span>
   139	
   140	  const person = resolvePerson(value)
   141	
   142	  // 2026-05-14 I1 fix(per codex addendum verdict):outer `inline-flex` → `flex w-full`
   143	  // 完成 truncate 寬度約束鏈。原 inline-flex content-width parent constrain 不到 name span
   144	  // → cell overflow-hidden 硬裁 → ellipsis dots 不可見。改 flex(block-level full width)
   145	  // + inner name span `flex-1 min-w-0 truncate` 真實 truncate-with-ellipsis 顯示。
   146	  // 對齊 GitHub Primer ActionList / Slack users_select / Atlassian UserPicker truncation canonical。
   147	  return (
   148	    <span className="flex items-start gap-2 min-w-0 w-full">
   149	      <ItemPrefix><PersonAvatar person={person} size={size} /></ItemPrefix>
   150	      <span className="truncate flex-1 min-w-0">{person.name}</span>
   151	    </span>
   152	  )
   153	}
   154	PersonDisplay.displayName = 'PersonDisplay'
   155	
   156	// ── Multi Person Display ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   157	// 多人堆疊:avatar 重疊(-2px),不顯示人名。
   158	// 第一個 avatar z-index 最高(在最上面),依此類推。
   159	// 溢出時顯示 +N 指示器,hover 出 tooltip 列出溢出的人(avatar + 人名)。
   160	
   161	function MultiPersonDisplay({
   162	  value,
   163	  size = 'md',
   164	  max,
   165	  measured = false,
   166	  onRemove,
   167	}: {
   168	  value?: PersonValue[] | null
   169	  size?: 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg'
   170	  /** 最多顯示幾個 avatar(不含 +N),預設 3。`measured=true` 時忽略此 prop(改 container width 算)*/
   171	  max?: number
   172	  /**
   173	   * 2026-05-15 codex Round 5 C+ SSOT fix:`measured=true` 啟動 container-width 量測(取代 hardcode `max ?? 3`)
   174	   * → display + edit stack 同 algorithm(同 cell width → 同 overflow 判斷),不再 display 用固定 3 vs edit
   175	   * 用 useOverflowCount。對齊 field-controls.spec.md:286 「4-mode 共享 renderer」contract + user round 3
   176	   * verbatim「同空間兩判斷點」SSOT directive。Default false 保 backward compat(non-cell context 仍 max ?? 3)。
   177	   */
   178	  measured?: boolean
   179	  /** 傳入時啟用 dismiss(edit mode),callback 接收被移除的 person */
   180	  onRemove?: (person: PersonValue) => void
   181	}) {
   182	  if (!value || value.length === 0) return <span className="text-fg-muted">{EMPTY_DISPLAY}</span>
   183	
   184	  // 2026-05-15 Bug 3 fix(Claude+Codex Step 5 比稿 consensus):消費 shared `avatar-stack-overflow`
   185	  // primitive。原 inline canvas-based formula 是 dual-implementation 違反 user SSOT「同 cell width 同
   186	  // overflow 判斷」(edit path 用 Combobox useOverflowCount DOM offsetWidth / display path 用 inline
   187	  // canvas)。**抽 primitive 統一**:display + edit 共用 `getAvatarStackVisibleCount` formula。
   188	  // SSOT in `./avatar-stack-overflow.ts`,M14 mechanical guard 防 future drift。
   189	  const containerRef = React.useRef<HTMLSpanElement>(null)
   190	  const [measuredCount, setMeasuredCount] = React.useState<number | null>(null)
   191	  React.useLayoutEffect(() => {
   192	    if (!measured) return
   193	    const el = containerRef.current
   194	    if (!el) return
   195	    const calc = () => {
   196	      const visible = getAvatarStackVisibleCount({
   197	        availablePx: el.clientWidth,
   198	        total: value.length,
   199	        avatarPx: AVATAR_STACK_AVATAR_PX[size],
   200	        overflowChipPx: AVATAR_STACK_OVERFLOW_CHIP_PX[size],
   201	      })
   202	      setMeasuredCount(visible)
   203	    }
   204	    calc()
   205	    const ro = new ResizeObserver(calc)
   206	    ro.observe(el)
   207	    return () => ro.disconnect()
   208	  }, [measured, size, value])
   209	
   210	  const resolvedMax = measured && measuredCount !== null ? measuredCount : (max ?? 3)
   211	  const people = value.map(resolvePerson)
   212	  const visible = people.slice(0, resolvedMax)
   213	  const hidden = people.slice(resolvedMax)
   214	  const overflow = hidden.length
   215	
   216	  // 單人回退到 PersonDisplay(顯示名字)
   217	  if (people.length === 1) {
   218	    return <PersonDisplay value={value[0]} size={size} />
   219	  }
   220	
   221	  // 2026-05-14 item-anatomy SSOT fix(per codex+Layer A 共識):outer items-start + avatar stack
   222	  // 鎖 first-line baseline(整 stack 是 prefix slot,h-[1lh] 對齊 first line)。
   223	  return (
   224	    <span ref={containerRef} className="inline-flex items-start min-w-0">
   225	      <ItemPrefix className="!justify-start"><span className="inline-flex items-center min-w-0">
   226	      {visible.map((person, i) => {
   227	        // **2026-05-07 v15.11 Bug D 升級 SSOT**:visible avatar 也支援 inline dismiss
   228	        // (對齊 user directive「avatar = tag」)。Dismiss overlay 走 `AvatarDismissOverlay`
   229	        // 共用 SSOT(下方 export),Combobox tagRenderer / 此處 / 任何 future avatar consumer
   230	        // 都用同一視覺 — 紅圈 X 對齊 avatar 右上,hover/focus-visible 才顯。
   231	        const handleDismiss = onRemove ? () => onRemove(value![i]) : undefined
   232	        return (
   233	          <span key={person.name + i} className={`relative inline-flex group/avatar ${i > 0 ? '-ml-0.5' : ''}`} style={{ zIndex: visible.length - i }}>
   234	            <PersonAvatar
   235	              person={person}
   236	              size={size}
   237	              className="ring-2 ring-[var(--surface)]"
   238	            />
   239	            {handleDismiss && <AvatarDismissOverlay onRemove={handleDismiss} label={person.name} />}
   240	          </span>

 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	/**
     2	 * avatar-stack-overflow — Deterministic SSOT primitive for avatar stack overflow math
     3	 *
     4	 * **2026-05-15 Bug 3 fix(Claude+Codex Step 5 比稿 consensus,user verbatim「就 A」)**:
     5	 *
     6	 * Real root cause of Bug 3「same cell width but different overflow timing per total count」:
     7	 *   1. `useOverflowCount` 在 Combobox 用 DOM `offsetWidth` 量測 + `overflowW = 60` fallback(實際 24px)
     8	 *   2. `overflowEl` 不被 ResizeObserver observe,first calc 用 fallback 後不會 recalc
     9	 *   3. `offsetWidth` 不減 `-ml-0.5` overlap → measurement 偏保守
    10	 *   4. **架構違反**:`MultiPersonDisplay` display path 用 canvas-based 算 / Combobox edit path 用 DOM offsetWidth
    11	 *      → 同 cell width 兩 path 不同結果 → user verbatim「同寬 cell overflow 時間不一樣」SSOT 根本被違反
    12	 *
    13	 * **Fix**(per codex Q3 consensus):抽 pure formula + React hook,display + edit 兩 path **共用**。
    14	 *
    15	 * **Deterministic formula**:
    16	 * ```
    17	 * firstAvatar + (visible - 1) * (avatar - overlap) + overflowChip <= available
    18	 * ```
    19	 * - `firstAvatar`:第一個 avatar 全寬 = `avatarPx`
    20	 * - subsequent items:`avatar - overlap`(stack `-ml-0.5` 視覺等同 measurement subtract)
    21	 * - `overflowChip`:若有 hidden,留 +N chip 空間;最後一個 visible item 不需留(`remaining === 0`)
    22	 *
    23	 * **Why centralize**:M14 mechanical guard against future drift。`MultiPersonDisplay` +
    24	 * PeoplePicker stack edit + future avatar consumers 都 import 此 helper,不可 copy formula。
    25	 * 對齊 codex「one avatar-stack primitive owns avatarPx, overlapPx, overflowChipPx」directive。
    26	 *
    27	 * **Benchmark cite**(per codex external baseline):MDN flex truncation / MUI Autocomplete
    28	 * limitTags / Ant Select maxTagCount="responsive"(explicit overflow contract,非 incidental clip)/
    29	 * Primer Truncate(parent-constrained max width)。
    30	 */
    31	
    32	/**
    33	 * Pure deterministic visible-count formula for avatar stack with overlap + overflow chip.
    34	 *
    35	 * @param availablePx — Container width available for the entire stack(含 +N chip 預留空間)
    36	 * @param total — Total avatars in selection
    37	 * @param avatarPx — Per-avatar pixel width(包含 ring border)
    38	 * @param overlapPx — Negative margin overlap between siblings(default 2px = `-ml-0.5`)
    39	 * @param overflowChipPx — Width reserved for +N indicator when overflow needed(default 24px = circle h-6 min-w-6)
    40	 * @returns visible count(0 ≤ visible ≤ total)。若全部 fit 則 visible = total(無 +N chip);否則 visible 為 max fit。
    41	 */
    42	export function getAvatarStackVisibleCount({
    43	  availablePx,
    44	  total,
    45	  avatarPx,
    46	  overlapPx = 2,
    47	  overflowChipPx = 24,
    48	}: {
    49	  availablePx: number
    50	  total: number
    51	  avatarPx: number
    52	  overlapPx?: number
    53	  overflowChipPx?: number
    54	}): number {
    55	  if (total <= 0 || availablePx <= 0) return 0
    56	  // First, check if 全部 fit without overflow chip(`remaining === 0` last item rule)
    57	  // 全部 fit: firstAvatar + (total-1) * (avatar - overlap) <= availablePx
    58	  const fullStackWidth = avatarPx + Math.max(0, total - 1) * (avatarPx - overlapPx)
    59	  if (fullStackWidth <= availablePx) return total
    60	
    61	  // 全部不 fit → 需 overflow chip。Find max visible N s.t.:
    62	  //   firstAvatar + (N - 1) * (avatar - overlap) + overflowChipPx <= availablePx
    63	  // Solve for N:
    64	  //   (N - 1) * (avatar - overlap) <= availablePx - firstAvatar - overflowChipPx
    65	  //   N - 1 <= (availablePx - firstAvatar - overflowChipPx) / (avatar - overlap)
    66	  //   N <= 1 + floor(...)
    67	  const step = avatarPx - overlapPx
    68	  if (step <= 0) return Math.min(total, 1)  // pathological case: full overlap or wider overlap
    69	  const remainder = availablePx - avatarPx - overflowChipPx
    70	  if (remainder < 0) return 0  // even 1 avatar + chip doesn't fit → 0 visible + +N
    71	  const visible = 1 + Math.floor(remainder / step)
    72	  return Math.max(0, Math.min(visible, total - 1))  // -1 because at least 1 must overflow when full stack doesn't fit
    73	}
    74	
    75	/**
    76	 * Map size token to avatar pixel(對齊 person-display.tsx:80 AVATAR_PX SSOT)。
    77	 */
    78	export const AVATAR_STACK_AVATAR_PX: Record<'sm' | 'md' | 'lg', number> = {
    79	  sm: 20,
    80	  md: 24,
    81	  lg: 24,
    82	}
    83	
    84	/**
    85	 * Default overflow chip width per size(對齊 overflow-indicator.tsx:17 triggerSize SSOT)。
    86	 * shape='circle' → h-{5|6} min-w-{5|6} ≈ 20-24px
    87	 */
    88	export const AVATAR_STACK_OVERFLOW_CHIP_PX: Record<'sm' | 'md' | 'lg', number> = {
    89	  sm: 20,
    90	  md: 24,
    91	  lg: 24,
    92	}

    77	  children: React.ReactNode
    78	  /** 搜尋框 placeholder */
    79	  searchPlaceholder?: string
    80	  /** 空選項提示 */
    81	  emptyText?: string
    82	  /** Loading 狀態(2026-05-15 audit B fix per user verbatim「dropdown 隨時可開,讀取在 panel 中間 CircularProgress」)
    83	   *  true → render `<Empty icon={<CircularProgress size={48}/>} description={loadingText} />` 取代 options;
    84	   *  trigger 不變,user 隨時可開 dropdown。對齊 MUI Autocomplete `loadingText` dropdown-body + Ant Select
    85	   *  loading idiom + DS 既有 `empty.spec.md:182` 「全頁 loading = Empty + CircularProgress compose」SSOT。
    86	   */
    87	  loading?: boolean
    88	
    89	  /** 尺寸 */
    90	  size?: SizeKey
    91	  /** 對齊方式 */
    92	  align?: 'start' | 'end'
    93	  /** 列表最少顯示幾行選項高度（預設 3），影響空狀態最小高度 */
    94	  minRows?: number
    95	  /** 最小寬度（px），預設跟隨觸發元件 */
    96	  minWidth?: number
    97	
    98	  /** 受控 open 狀態 */
    99	  open?: boolean
   100	  /** 預設打開(uncontrolled initial state)— 2026-05-15 audit Dim 26 V1 fix per user verbatim「A:1」approval */
   101	  defaultOpen?: boolean
   102	  /** open 狀態變更 callback */
   103	  onOpenChange?: (open: boolean) => void
   104	
   105	  /** 自訂選項 label 渲染（預設渲染 option.label 純文字） */
   106	  renderLabel?: (option: SelectMenuOption) => React.ReactNode
   107	  /** 攔截 PopoverContent 的 onOpenAutoFocus（如 Select searchable 需阻止 focus 搶走） */
   108	  onOpenAutoFocus?: (e: Event) => void
   109	
   110	  /**
   111	   * Popover 內容容器的 DOM id。Combobox / 自定 trigger 用 `aria-controls` 指向此 id 時,
   112	   * 需傳入相同 id 讓 AT 能找到對應的 listbox。
   113	   */
   114	  contentId?: string
   115	
   116	  className?: string
   117	}
   118	
   119	// shadcn canonical:forwardRef + displayName 統一。SelectMenu 是 Popover + Command
   120	// composite,自身無 DOM host(trigger 由 consumer 以 asChild children 提供),ref 簽名
   121	// 保留但不附著(consumer 想取 trigger DOM 直接在 children 上自己 ref)。className 合併到
   122	// PopoverContent(contextually 最接近 user-facing surface)。
   123	const SelectMenu = React.forwardRef<HTMLElement, SelectMenuProps>(function SelectMenu({
   124	  options,
   125	  groups,
   126	  value,
   127	  onValueChange,
   128	  multiple = false,
   129	  searchable = false,
   130	  creatable = false,
   131	  onCreate,
   132	  createLabel = (q) => `直接使用「${q}」`,
   133	  children,
   134	  searchPlaceholder = '搜尋…', // i18n-allow: DS default; consumer override via searchPlaceholder prop
   135	  emptyText = '沒有符合的選項', // i18n-allow: DS default; consumer override via emptyText prop
   136	  loading = false,
   137	  size = 'md',
   138	  align = 'start',
   139	  minRows = 3,
   140	  minWidth,
   141	  open: controlledOpen,
   142	  defaultOpen,
   143	  onOpenChange: controlledOnOpenChange,
   144	  renderLabel,
   145	  onOpenAutoFocus,
   146	  contentId,
   147	  className,
   148	}, _ref) {
   149	  // ── State ──
   150	  const [internalOpen, setInternalOpen] = React.useState(defaultOpen ?? false)
   151	  const open = controlledOpen ?? internalOpen
   152	  const setOpen = controlledOnOpenChange ?? setInternalOpen
   153	  const [search, setSearch] = React.useState('')
   154	
   155	  // ── Value helpers ──
   156	  const selectedValues = React.useMemo<string[]>(() => {
   157	    if (value == null) return []
   158	    return Array.isArray(value) ? value : [value]
   159	  }, [value])
   160	
   161	  const isSelected = React.useCallback(
   162	    (v: string) => selectedValues.includes(v),
   163	    [selectedValues]
   164	  )
   165	
   166	  const handleSelect = React.useCallback(
   167	    (optionValue: string) => {
   168	      if (multiple) {
   169	        const next = isSelected(optionValue)
   170	          ? selectedValues.filter((v) => v !== optionValue)
   171	          : [...selectedValues, optionValue]
   172	        onValueChange?.(next)
   173	      } else {
   174	        onValueChange?.(optionValue)
   175	        setOpen(false)
   176	      }
   177	    },
   178	    [multiple, selectedValues, isSelected, onValueChange, setOpen]
   179	  )
   180	
   181	  // ── Multi-select: select all ──
   182	  const selectableOptions = React.useMemo(
   183	    () => options.filter((o) => !o.disabled),
   184	    [options]
   185	  )
   186	
   187	  const allState: boolean | 'indeterminate' = React.useMemo(() => {
   188	    if (!multiple) return false
   189	    const count = selectableOptions.filter((o) => isSelected(o.value)).length
   190	    if (count === 0) return false
   191	    if (count === selectableOptions.length) return true
   192	    return 'indeterminate'
   193	  }, [multiple, selectableOptions, isSelected])
   194	
   195	  const handleSelectAll = React.useCallback(() => {
   196	    if (!multiple) return
   197	    if (allState === true) {
   198	      onValueChange?.([])
   199	    } else {
   200	      onValueChange?.(selectableOptions.map((o) => o.value))
   201	    }
   202	  }, [multiple, allState, selectableOptions, onValueChange])
   203	
   204	  // ── Creatable ──
   205	  const showCreate = React.useMemo(() => {
   206	    if (!creatable || !search.trim()) return false
   207	    return !options.some(
   208	      (o) => o.label.toLowerCase() === search.trim().toLowerCase()
   209	    )
   210	  }, [creatable, search, options])
   211	
   212	  // ── Grouping ──
   213	  const groupedOptions = React.useMemo(() => {
   214	    if (!groups?.length) return [{ key: '__default', label: '', options }]
   215	    const grouped = groups.map((g) => ({
   216	      ...g,
   217	      options: options.filter((o) => o.group === g.key),
   218	    }))
   219	    const ungrouped = options.filter((o) => !o.group)
   220	    if (ungrouped.length) {

    15	
    16	# PeoplePicker 設計原則
    17	
    18	## 定位
    19	
    20	PeoplePicker 是**人員選擇器**——專為「從人員清單中選一個或多個」設計的複合元件。外觀對齊 Select / Combobox，差異在選項前綴有 Avatar 視覺。
    21	
    22	**實作基礎**：組合元件——Popover + Command（cmdk）搜尋 + SelectMenu 浮層 + PersonDisplay render。無直接 external primitive base（底層靠 shadcn passthrough 的 Popover / Command）。
    23	
    24	共用規則見 `../Field/field-controls.spec.md`。本文件只記錄 PeoplePicker 特有的原則。
    25	
    26	**Layout Family**：CLAUDE.md 4-Family Model **Family 4（Field control layout）** 消費者。結構繼承 `components/Field/field-controls.spec.md` 的 `fieldWrapperStyles + [startIcon?] [<editable>] [endAction?]` 規格,視覺對齊 Family 1（Menu item）讓 SelectMenu trigger + options 連續一致。
    27	
    28	---
    29	
    30	## 何時用
    31	
    32	- **指派人員**：指派 task、assignee、reviewer 選擇
    33	- **加入成員**：team / channel / project 加人
    34	- **@提及選擇器**：文章 / 留言 / chat 內插入 @user
    35	- **多人協作選擇**：訂單協作人員、共同擁有者
    36	- **需要 avatar 視覺識別**：人員清單視覺辨識高於純文字 label
    37	
    38	## 何時不用
    39	
    40	| 場景 | 改用 | 原因 |
    41	|------|------|------|
    42	| 一般分類選擇（非人員）| `Select` / `Combobox` | PeoplePicker 專為人員設計，有 Avatar prefix |
    43	| 單選純文字選項（狀態 / 類別）| `Select` | PeoplePicker 開銷較大，靠 Avatar 識別；非人員用 Select |
    44	| 多選非人員 tag | `Combobox` | Combobox 是通用多選，無 Avatar 假設 |
    45	| 只顯示單一人員（不需選擇）| `NameCard` + `Avatar` | PeoplePicker 是選擇器，純展示用 NameCard |
    46	| 顯示整個 team 成員列表 | `Avatar.Group` / 自訂 list | PeoplePicker 是「選人」介面，不是「展示 team」 |
    47	
    48	---
    49	
    50	## 單選 vs 多選
    51	
    52	透過 `value` prop 的類型決定：
    53	
    54	| 模式 | value 類型 | 視覺 |
    55	|------|-----------|------|
    56	| 單選 | `PersonValue \| null` | Field 顯示單一 Avatar + Name |
    57	| 多選 | `PersonValue[]` | Field 顯示 Avatar 陣列（與 Combobox 多選同模式）|
    58	
    59	**判斷**：
    60	- 「這個 task 指派給誰」→ 單選（assignee 通常一個）
    61	- 「選擇 reviewers」→ 多選（reviewer 可多人）
    62	- 「加入 channel 的成員」→ 多選
    63	- 「文章作者」→ 單選
    64	
    65	---
    66	
    67	## 搜尋
    68	
    69	PeoplePicker 永遠支援搜尋（內部使用 `Command` / cmdk）——因為人員清單通常規模較大且使用者記得人名關鍵字（符合 Select spec「Searchable 開啟判斷」的「label 性質」主判準：人名是獨特關鍵字）。
    70	
    71	- **搜尋 placeholder**：預設「搜尋人員…」，可透過 `searchPlaceholder` 覆寫
    72	- **空狀態**：預設「沒有符合的人員」，透過 `emptyText` 覆寫
    73	
    74	---
    75	
    76	## 與 Select / Combobox 的分界
    77	
    78	| | PeoplePicker | Select | Combobox |
    79	|---|---|---|---|
    80	| 資料類型 | **人員**（含 Avatar） | 任意（純文字）| 任意（純文字）|
    81	| 單選 / 多選 | 兩者皆支援（value 類型決定）| 單選 | 多選 |
    82	| 視覺 prefix | Avatar（必備） | 可選 startIcon | 無 |
    83	| 底層實作 | Popover + Command + SelectMenu | native `<select>` | native `<select>` + Tag overlay |
    84	| 搜尋 | 永遠啟用（人名本質）— 走 inline-trigger | 可選 `searchable`（單選短列表 → inline-trigger only）| 可選 `searchable` + `searchIn='menu' \| 'trigger'`（多選 → 兩種模式）|
    85	
    86	**搜尋型態 SSOT canonical**（A1-A5 spec,2026-05-11;2026-05-12 補 PeoplePicker multi `searchIn` opt-in）：
    87	
    88	| 型態 | 使用情境 | 元件 API |
    89	|---|---|---|
    90	| **none** | 短列表 (< 7 選項) / 自然語言 label 可用 native type-ahead | 不傳 `searchable` |
    91	| **inline-trigger** | 單選 + 需快速 type-and-pick;trigger 變 input | `<Select searchable />` / `<Combobox searchable searchIn='trigger' />` / `<PeoplePicker />` single / `<PeoplePicker multi searchIn='trigger' />` |
    92	| **panel-top** | 多選 + 連續 type-and-select(關鍵字保留在 menu 不被 chip 切走) | `<Combobox searchable searchIn='menu' />` / `<PeoplePicker multi />`(default menu) |
    93	
    94	### Trigger display SSOT canonical table(2026-05-15 v3 user verbatim 整理)
    95	
    96	**PeoplePicker 是獨立元件,有自己的另一層 SSOT,並非完全繼承 Select / Combobox**。下表標出哪些繼承、哪些 PeoplePicker 自己定義 — **改一處先看本表,違反該層 SSOT = 漂移**。
    97	
    98	#### A. 元件本質繼承表
    99	
   100	| 面向 | 來源 SSOT |
   101	|---|---|
   102	| 單人互動邏輯(open/close/keyboard/搜尋)| **繼承 Select**(只多套一層 Avatar 視覺包裝)|
   103	| 多人互動邏輯(N tag / overflow / inline-search)| **繼承 Combobox**(但 tag 和溢出**換成圓形 avatar 視覺**)|
   104	| Avatar 在 field 內 padding(12px 固定)| **PeoplePicker 自己**(不繼承 Combobox density-dependent 公式)|
   105	| +N 溢出 chip 形狀(**圓形**)| **PeoplePicker 自己**(不繼承 Combobox 矩形 tag) |
   106	| 多人 tag 視覺(**圓形 avatar overlap `-ml-0.5`**) | **PeoplePicker 自己**(不繼承 Combobox 矩形 Tag chip)|
   107	| 多人 length=1 視覺(降階為 avatar+人名,跟單人視覺一致)| **PeoplePicker 自己**(Combobox 無此特殊)|
   108	
   109	#### B. 單人完整 trigger SSOT
   110	
   111	| state | trigger 顯示 |
   112	|---|---|
   113	| 空、closed | placeholder「請選擇人員」+ 按空間 ellipsis |
   114	| 選 1 人、closed | avatar + 人名 + 按空間 ellipsis(`PersonDisplay`,`person-display.tsx:131-147`)|
   115	| open + inline-search、未選 | input cursor + placeholder「請選擇人員」(trigger empty placeholder,**不**用「搜尋…」)|
   116	| open + inline-search、選 1 人 | input cursor + placeholder = **該人名**(本人名字當搜尋預設值,按空間 ellipsis;`select.tsx:185` `selectedLabel \|\| placeholder` empty-state fallback canonical)|
   117	| open + panel-search、選 1 人 | avatar + 人名 + ellipsis(搜尋框在 panel 內,trigger 視覺不變)|
   118	
   119	#### C. 多人 length=1 trigger SSOT(降階為單人視覺)
   120	
   121	| state | trigger 顯示 |
   122	|---|---|
   123	| closed | avatar + 人名 + ellipsis(= 單人 closed,共享 `PersonDisplay`)|
   124	| open + panel-search | avatar + 人名 + ellipsis(panel 內搜尋,trigger 視覺不變)|
   125	| open + inline-search | avatar + **input cursor**(原本人名位置被輸入區取代;**因 avatar 仍可見,placeholder 永遠空,只剩 cursor** — 對齊 §E 「avatar 存在 → placeholder 空」rule,避免視覺重複造成混亂)|
   126	
   127	#### D. 多人 length≥2 trigger SSOT(avatar stack 視覺)
   128	
   129	| state | trigger 顯示 |
   130	|---|---|
   131	| closed | **圓形 avatar stack overlap `-ml-0.5` + 圓形 +N 溢出 chip**(本來放人名的地方不放人名)|
   132	| open + inline-search、**未選**(length=0)| input cursor + placeholder「請選擇人員」(trigger empty placeholder,**不**用「搜尋…」)|
   133	| open + inline-search、**已選**(length≥2)| **avatar stack + 圓形 +N + input cursor 在 +N 的右側**(stack 跟 +N 不動;cursor 接在 +N 後;empty search 不顯 placeholder,純 cursor。對齊 Combobox `trailing` slot placement)|
   134	| open + panel-search、已選 | avatar stack + 圓形 +N(searchbox 在 panel 內,trigger 視覺不變)|
   135	
   136	#### E. 共享 SSOT(單人 ↔ 多人 length=1 必對齊)
   137	
   138	| 共享項 | SSOT owner |
   139	|---|---|
   140	| Avatar 左 inset 距 trigger.left = 12px 固定(不隨 size/density 漂移)| 本 spec L94 + `people-picker.tsx:316` `!px-3` inject(form context)/ `!px-[var(--table-cell-px)]`(naked variant table cell)|
   141	| Avatar+人名視覺 | `person-display.tsx:131-147` `PersonDisplay`(共享 renderer)|
   142	| 人名按空間 ellipsis | `person-display.tsx:144` `truncate flex-1 min-w-0` |
   143	| Placeholder ellipsis(inline-search active 時)| `field-wrapper.tsx:244` `bareInputStyles` 含 `truncate` |
   144	| Empty-state inline-search placeholder(未選時 → trigger empty placeholder) | `select.tsx:185` `selectedLabel \|\| placeholder` / `combobox.tsx:554` `items.length === 0 ? placeholder : ''`(2026-05-15 Drift A fix 對齊 PeoplePicker SSOT)|
   145	
   146	**Avatar-presence → placeholder 規則(2026-05-15 user verbatim「只要有 avatar 存在,placeholder 都是空的,只會出現 cursor,這樣才不會造成混亂」)**:
   147	
   148	| 場景 | avatar 是否可見 | placeholder 行為 |
   149	|---|---|---|
   150	| 單人 inline-search、已選、open | ❌(input **取代** avatar/name,avatar 消失)| placeholder = **selectedLabel(該人名,memory aid)** — `select.tsx:185` |
   151	| 單人 inline-search、未選、open | ❌(從來沒 avatar)| placeholder = **trigger empty placeholder「請選擇人員」** |
   152	| 多人 inline-search、length≥1、open | ✅(avatar/stack 仍在,input 在 trailing)| **placeholder = '' 純 cursor**(避免跟 avatar 重複)|
   153	| 多人 inline-search、length=0、open | ❌(empty)| placeholder = **trigger empty placeholder「請選擇人員」** — `combobox.tsx:554`(Drift A fix)|
   154	
   155	**規則一句話**:`placeholder = (visible_avatar_exists) ? '' : (selectedLabel ?? triggerEmptyPlaceholder)`。
   156	
   157	**搜尋預設模式(2026-05-15 user 拍板)**:多選系列 default `searchIn='menu'`(panel-top search)。`searchIn='trigger'` 為 opt-in。Single mode 永遠 inline-search(Select 慣例)。
   158	
   159	#### F. Cell-edit ↔ Field-edit 一致性 invariant
   160	
   161	`MultiPersonCell` / `PersonCell`(`cell-registry.tsx:381-391` cell-as-input)+ form context PeoplePicker **包同一個元件**,所以 §B/§C/§D 規則對兩 surface 都成立。差別只在 padding 機制(共 §E)— 兩 surface 都產出 12px inset,**禁分歧**。
   162	
   163	**改 PeoplePicker 視覺前必查本表,動 trigger render / placeholder / overflowShape / tagWrapperClassName 前先 cite 對應 row。** Hook `check_peoplepicker_ssot_drift.sh` 機械強制。
   164	
   165	**Avatar 左 inset SSOT(2026-05-13 v2 — user 拍 Path a + density-drift root-cause,GitHub people picker idiom)**:single trigger / multi stack 第一個 avatar 距 trigger.left = **12px 固定**(不隨 size / density 漂移)。實作:PeoplePicker form context + 有 tag → `cn(className, '!px-3')` inject 12px override 到 Combobox Field wrapper,**覆蓋** Combobox `tagPadding[size]` density-dependent calc 公式;`tagAreaPaddingLeftPx={undefined}` 不再 +8 magic。Cell context naked variant `!px-[var(--table-cell-px)]` 已是 12px 不 inject。**為何 v1「4+8=12」公式報廢**(per 2026-05-13 codex V2 verdict correction):`tagPadding[size]` 是 `(field-height - icon-size) / 2`,真值表:default sm/md=4px → 4+8=12 ✓;default lg=6px → 14px ✗;comfortable sm/md=6px → 14px ✗;comfortable lg=8px → 16px ✗。**default sm + default md 兩個 size 也 = 12px**(我前 too narrow claim「只 md」 codex 修正);**真正漂的 = default lg + 全 comfortable 共 4 個組合**。整體 stale 結論不變(4 個漂 / 2 個對),故 `!px-3` 固定 12px 是正解。對齊 GitHub picker / Material Autocomplete renderTags / Ant Select tagRender 共享 fixed-inset canonical(不 scale with size)。
   166	
   167	**判準**：
   168	- **選人 → PeoplePicker**（不用 Select / Combobox 代替，失去 Avatar 視覺）
   169	- **非人員單選 → Select**
   170	- **非人員多選 → Combobox**
   171	
   172	---
   173	
   174	## PersonValue 型別
   175	
   176	```tsx
   177	type PersonValue = string | { name: string; avatarUrl?: string; description?: string }
   178	```
   179	
   180	- **簡單用 string**：只有名字（fallback 顯示 initials）
   181	- **完整物件**：包含 avatar URL 和 description（顯示 Avatar + 次要資訊如 role / email）
   182	
   183	---
   184	
   185	## readonly / disabled
   186	
   187	與其他 Field 一致：
   188	- **readonly**：顯示選中人員（Avatar + Name），無 dropdown trigger、無搜尋
   189	- **disabled**：灰化整個 field，不可互動
   190	
   191	---
   192	
   193	## 禁止事項
   194	
   195	- ❌ 用 PeoplePicker 選非人員（部門 / 專案 / 類別）——那些用 Select / Combobox
   196	- ❌ 在 readonly 模式顯示搜尋或 dropdown——readonly 是純展示
   197	- ❌ 多選情境強制單選（限制 value.length === 1）——改用 Select（如果真的單選）
   198	- ❌ 把 PeoplePicker 當 Team Member 展示元件用（不選人、只看名單）——用 Avatar.Group 或自訂 list
   199	- ❌ 不搭配 Avatar 視覺（純文字名字）——失去 PeoplePicker 存在的理由，直接用 Select / Combobox
   200	
   201	---
   202	
   203	## 為何無 Inspector
   204	
   205	PeoplePicker 是 **composite Field Control**(Field shell + Avatar + SelectMenu),關鍵決策維度是 `mode`(single / multi)× `size` × search behavior × value type——已由 `ModeMatrix` / `SizeMatrix` / `ColorMatrix` / `StateBehavior` / `PersonValueType` 五張矩陣完整覆蓋。互動 Inspector 對 composite 元件較弱:「傳 PersonValue 陣列」需要真實資料 fixture 展示,單組合試玩無法呈現——改以 `StateBehavior` 的真實 Assignee picker 場景取代。
   206	
   207	對應 anatomy story:保留 `Overview` + 元件特有 `ModeMatrix` / `PersonValueType` + `SizeMatrix` + `ColorMatrix` + `StateBehavior`。
   208	
   209	---
   210	
   211	## shadcn passthrough 例外說明
   212	
   213	PeoplePicker 是 **composite 元件**(Popover + Command + SelectMenu + Avatar 內部組裝),其 API 為完全 declarative(value / onChange / size / mode / options...)。**不套 `forwardRef` / `...props` spread**:
   214	
   215	- **沒有單一 DOM root 可 ref**:consumer「對誰 forward」含糊——指 Popover trigger?Command search input?SelectMenu content?任一選擇都會誤導 consumer
   216	- **`...props` spread 會撒到何處?** composite 元件無 identity DOM,spread 若到 root wrapper 多半無意義(wrapper 只是 flex container);到 trigger 則語義不清
   217	- **API 邊界明確才是 composite 價值**:PeoplePicker 暴露的是「選人」語意,不是「彈出選單 + 搜尋 + 渲染頭像」的 DOM 細節。若 consumer 需要 DOM-level 控制,該用底層 Popover + Combobox 自組,不該透過 PeoplePicker
   218	
   219	`displayName = 'PeoplePicker'` 保留,無 `asChild`(composite 不是 Slot-compat)。
   220	
   221	---

   250	## Display — 格式化顯示
   251	
   252	每個 Field 元件 export 一個 Display 子元件，負責把 raw value 格式化為可讀文字或 ReactNode。
   253	
   254	Display 的消費者：
   255	- **DataTable cell**：根據 `meta.type` 自動選擇對應的 Display 元件
   256	- **Field readonly 模式**：內部使用相同的格式化邏輯
   257	
   258	### null / undefined 值
   259	
   260	Display 模式統一顯示 em dash `—`，顏色 `text-fg-muted`。edit 模式顯示空白。
   261	
   262	此規則適用於所有 Field 類型，boolean 例外（顯示 unchecked 狀態）。
   263	
   264	### DataTable 整合
   265	
   266	DataTable 根據 column 的 `meta.type` 自動選擇 Display 元件：
   267	
   268	```tsx
   269	// 自動渲染——不需要手寫 cell
   270	col.accessor('price', {
   271	  header: 'Price',
   272	  meta: { type: 'currency', prefix: '$' },
   273	})
   274	
   275	// 客製化——有自訂 cell 時完全跳過 type → Display
   276	col.accessor('status', {
   277	  header: 'Status',
   278	  cell: (info) => <MyCustomBadge status={info.getValue()} />,
   279	})
   280	```
   281	
   282	兩者可在同一張 table 混用。
   283	
   284	---
   285	
   286	## 共享 contract(2026-05-12 Stream C — Selected renderer / Placeholder vocabulary / Cell surface)
   287	
   288	**(a) Selected value renderer**:rich display(avatar+name/icon+label)元件**必**提供 consumer renderer slot,**display/readonly/disabled/edit** 4 mode 共享同一 renderer(禁 edit-only)。`Select.selectedItemRenderer` / `Combobox.tagRenderer`(edit 已接;display path unify deferred 下 cycle)/ PeoplePicker 走 `PersonDisplay`+`MultiPersonDisplay`+`Combobox.tagRenderer`。對齊 MUI Autocomplete `renderValue` / Ant Select `tagRender`+`labelRender`+`optionRender` / MUI DataGrid `renderCell`+`renderEditCell` 共享 params。
   289	
   290	**(b) Placeholder vocabulary**(3 props 對 3 UI state,**不可混用**):
   291	- `placeholder` — trigger empty(沒選值,例「請選擇人員」)— Ant/Polaris/Carbon canonical
   292	- `searchPlaceholder` — search input hint(例「搜尋人員…」)— Ant `searchPlaceholder`
   293	- `emptyText`/`noResultsText` — filtered menu 無結果(例「沒有符合的人員」)— Ant `notFoundContent` / Material X `localeText.noResultsOverlayLabel`
   294	
   295	**禁**:wrapper 把 `emptyText`(search-empty)silent forward 成 `emptyPlaceholder`(trigger-empty);**Combobox `emptyPlaceholder` deprecated**,保留 1 cycle fallback,future `placeholder` 唯一 trigger source。Hook `check_field_controls_contracts.sh` (contract b) 機械強制。
   296	
   297	**(c) Cell surface metrics**:Field family 在 cell 內**禁** hardcode padding(`tagAreaPaddingLeftPx={isEmpty ? undefined : 8}` 反 pattern)。改 **`FieldSurface` context**(`'form' | 'toolbar' | 'table-cell'`):`useFieldSurface()` 取值,`<FieldSurfaceProvider surface="table-cell">` 自動套於 `cell-registry.resolveCellComponent`。Consumer 用 `surface === 'table-cell'` 顯式 query(取代 `variant === 'naked'` heuristic)。**risk mitigation**:`avatar.left = cell.left + computed(--table-cell-px)`,禁再加 magic 8px(double-count)。**Token scope**:`--table-cell-px/py` 是 DataTable-scoped metric(CSS 定義在 `data-table.css`,Field naked variant 是 DataTable cell substrate sub-component 故 cross-path reference 不算真 cross-component),per 2026-05-13 codex Q2 verdict + AG Grid `cellHorizontalPadding`(grid theme param)/ MUI X `cellClassName`(per-cell)/ Carbon spacing scale primitive(不升 cell padding 全域 token)idiom — **不**升 `tokens/layoutSpace/` canonical。對齊 AG Grid cellRendererSelector / Material X DataGrid 共享 params / Notion property type registry。Hook `check_field_controls_contracts.sh` (contract c) 機械強制。
   298	
   299	**(d) Default variant display = zero chrome SSOT**(2026-05-13 user 拍板 Path Ⅰ + codex V2 verdict):default `mode='display'` **必** zero chrome。Display 純展示語意,真要包 chrome 走 `readonly` 或 `showDisplayEndIcon=true` opt-in。**Impl**:`field-wrapper.tsx` + `textarea.tsx` compoundVariants `mode:'display'+variant:'default'` 加 `!px-0 !py-0`。對齊 Carbon read-only / Stripe display / Notion property / Polaris readonly。Hook `check_field_controls_contracts.sh` (contract d) propose。
   300	
   301	**(e) Display typography canonical**(2026-05-14 user I2 + codex M31 verdict):Field family display path **必** consume `fieldWrapperStyles` size variants typography token — `sm/md → text-body`(14px line-height 1.5)/ `lg → text-body-lg`(16px)。**禁**:LinkInput / Select / Combobox 非 D-path 的 bare-span 直接 render 無 font-size class(瀏覽器 default 字體);**必**包 `text-body` (sm/md) / `text-body-lg` (lg) class。對齊跨 Field family display 視覺尺寸統一(user 抓 LinkInput display 字體跟其他 Field 不一致 = SSOT 違反 漏接 typography token)。**Impl**:LinkInput / Select / Combobox / DatePicker / TimePicker non-D-path bare-span 加 size-aware text class。world-class cite:MUI X DataGrid `Typography` consistent / Atlassian @atlaskit/textfield size-prop typography token / Polaris TextField typographyToken size-aware。
   302	
   303	---

    34	  // Constrain max-w-xs section to narrowPx
    35	  if (narrowPx) {
    36	    await page.addStyleTag({ content: `.max-w-xs { max-width: ${narrowPx}px !important; }` })
    37	    await page.waitForTimeout(500)
    38	  }
    39	
    40	  if (clickToOpen) {
    41	    const trigger = await page.locator('[role="combobox"]').first()
    42	    if (await trigger.count() > 0) {
    43	      await trigger.click()
    44	      await page.waitForTimeout(800)
    45	    }
    46	  }
    47	
    48	  const info = await page.evaluate(() => {
    49	    const trigger = document.querySelector('[role="combobox"]')
    50	    if (!trigger) return { error: 'no trigger' }
    51	    const rect = trigger.getBoundingClientRect()
    52	    const personImgs = trigger.querySelectorAll('img[alt]')
    53	    const truncSpans = trigger.querySelectorAll('[class*="truncate"]')
    54	    const overflowBtn = trigger.querySelector('[aria-label*="more"], button[aria-label*="位"]')
    55	    const truncs = Array.from(truncSpans).map(s => ({
    56	      text: s.textContent?.slice(0, 30) || '',
    57	      scrollW: s.scrollWidth,
    58	      clientW: s.clientWidth,
    59	      truncated: s.scrollWidth > s.clientWidth,
    60	    }))
    61	    return {
    62	      triggerWidth: Math.round(rect.width),
    63	      personAvatarCount: personImgs.length,
    64	      truncs,
    65	      hasOverflow: !!overflowBtn,
    66	      overflowText: overflowBtn?.textContent || '',
    67	    }
    68	  })
    69	  const screenshotPath = path.join(SNAPSHOTS_DIR, `${testId}.png`)
    70	  await page.screenshot({ path: screenshotPath, fullPage: false, clip: { x: 0, y: 0, width: 800, height: 400 } }).catch(() => {})
    71	  results.push({ testId, description, narrowPx, clickToOpen, ...info })
    72	  await page.close()
    73	}
    74	
    75	// Bug 1 + Bug 3:multi length=4 with long names, narrow trigger constraint
    76	// samplePeople first 4 = ['Alice Wonderland Wang', 'Bob Christopher Chen', 'Charlie Wu', 'Alexander Hamilton Zhang'] (per PeoplePicker stories typical sample data)
    77	await captureFullPeoplePickerMulti('Bug3-multi-default-wide', 'Multi length=4 default wide trigger (~320px max-w-xs)', null, false)
    78	await captureFullPeoplePickerMulti('Bug3-multi-narrow-180', 'Multi length=4 with 180px narrow trigger (simulate cell)', 180, false)
    79	await captureFullPeoplePickerMulti('Bug3-multi-narrow-120', 'Multi length=4 with 120px very narrow trigger', 120, false)
    80	await captureFullPeoplePickerMulti('Bug3-multi-narrow-180-opened', 'Multi length=4 narrow 180px + open panel-search', 180, true)
    81	
    82	// Bug 1 length=1 long name in narrow cell
    83	async function captureMultiLength1(testId, narrowPx) {
    84	  const page = await browser.newPage({ viewport: { width: 800, height: 600 } })
    85	  await page.goto(`${STORYBOOK_URL}/iframe.html?id=design-system-components-peoplepicker-展示--multi&viewMode=story`, { waitUntil: 'networkidle' }).catch(() => {})
    86	  await page.waitForTimeout(1500)
    87	  // Reduce to 1 selected by clicking checkboxes
    88	  const trigger = await page.locator('[role="combobox"]').first()
    89	  await trigger.click()
    90	  await page.waitForTimeout(600)
    91	  // Uncheck 3 to get length=1 (keeping Bob Christopher Chen for visible long name)
    92	  for (let i = 0; i < 3; i++) {
    93	    await page.evaluate(() => {
    94	      const items = document.querySelectorAll('[role="option"]')
    95	      for (const item of items) {
    96	        const checkbox = item.querySelector('[role="checkbox"]')
    97	        if (checkbox && checkbox.getAttribute('data-state') === 'checked') {
    98	          item.dispatchEvent(new MouseEvent('click', { bubbles: true }))
    99	          return true
   100	        }
   101	      }
   102	      return false
   103	    })
   104	    await page.waitForTimeout(300)
   105	  }
   106	  // Close popover
   107	  await page.mouse.click(400, 500)
   108	  await page.waitForTimeout(500)
   109	  if (narrowPx) {
   110	    await page.addStyleTag({ content: `.max-w-xs { max-width: ${narrowPx}px !important; }` })
   111	    await page.waitForTimeout(300)
   112	  }
   113	  const info = await page.evaluate(() => {
   114	    const trigger = document.querySelector('[role="combobox"]')
   115	    if (!trigger) return { error: 'no trigger' }
   116	    const rect = trigger.getBoundingClientRect()
   117	    const truncSpans = trigger.querySelectorAll('[class*="truncate"]')
   118	    const truncs = Array.from(truncSpans).map(s => ({
   119	      text: s.textContent?.slice(0, 30) || '',
   120	      scrollW: s.scrollWidth,
   121	      clientW: s.clientWidth,
   122	      truncated: s.scrollWidth > s.clientWidth,
   123	    }))
   124	    return { triggerWidth: Math.round(rect.width), truncs }
   125	  })
   126	  const screenshotPath = path.join(SNAPSHOTS_DIR, `Bug1-multi-length1-narrow-${narrowPx ?? 'default'}.png`)
   127	  await page.screenshot({ path: screenshotPath, fullPage: false, clip: { x: 0, y: 0, width: 800, height: 200 } }).catch(() => {})
   128	  results.push({ testId: `Bug1-multi-length1-${narrowPx ?? 'default'}`, description: `Multi length=1 with ${narrowPx ?? 'default'}px trigger`, ...info })
   129	  await page.close()
   130	}
   131	
   132	await captureMultiLength1('Bug1', null)
   133	await captureMultiLength1('Bug1-narrow', 180)
   134	await captureMultiLength1('Bug1-very-narrow', 120)
   135	
   136	await browser.close()
   137	
   138	fs.writeFileSync(REPORT_PATH, JSON.stringify({ ts: new Date().toISOString(), results }, null, 2))
   139	
   140	console.log('=== Real verify ===')

## Step 2 Verify 結果

**Bug A: agree Layer A.**  
`Combobox` public wrapper drops the forwarded ref:

- `src/design-system/components/Combobox/combobox.tsx:642-647`: `(props, _ref)` never passes `_ref`.
- `NativeCombobox` / `CustomCombobox` are plain functions at `combobox.tsx:408` and `combobox.tsx:472`, so there is no hidden internal ref forwarding.
- PeoplePicker stack depends on that ref: `people-picker.tsx:336-344` reads `stackContainerRef.current`, then returns early when null.
- Therefore `visibleCountOverride={stackVisibleCount}` at `people-picker.tsx:419-421` remains `undefined`, and `OverflowTagList` falls back to `useOverflowCount` at `combobox.tsx:171-174`.

**Bug B: agree Layer A.**  
`select.tsx:208-215` puts `inline-flex items-center truncate` on the same overlay span containing raw text. CSS evidence:

- W3C CSS Overflow says `text-overflow` applies to block containers and demonstrates block-container ellipsis behavior: https://www.w3.org/TR/css-overflow-3/#text-overflow
- MDN: `text-overflow` needs overflow/nowrap and affects content overflowing a block container: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/CSS/Reference/Properties/text-overflow
- Mozilla layout bug discussion confirms flex containers wrap raw text in an anonymous flex item; `text-overflow` must be on the text’s block container, which is anonymous and not styleable: https://bugzilla.mozilla.org/show_bug.cgi?id=972664#c1

`npx tsc -b`: **not clean-verifiable in this sandbox**. It failed only because read-only sandbox blocked writing `node_modules/.tmp/*.tsbuildinfo`.  
Fallback checks passed:

- `npx tsc -p tsconfig.app.json --noEmit --incremental false`
- `npx tsc -p tsconfig.node.json --noEmit --incremental false`

## Step 3 Visual

Layer C visual **missing**. `localhost:6006` was not running, and starting a static server from `storybook-static` failed with `PermissionError: [Errno 1] Operation not permitted` due sandbox network/bind restrictions. Layer A must run reproduce + screenshot verification.

## Step 4 Propose

| Root cause hypothesis | spec.md / source path:line / 引文 | Reasoning |
|---|---|---|
| Combobox public `forwardRef` drops ref, breaking PeoplePicker stack measurement | `combobox.tsx:642-647` uses `_ref` and renders `<NativeCombobox {...props} />` / `<CustomCombobox {...props} />`; `people-picker.tsx:343-344` `const root = stackContainerRef.current; if (!root) return`; `avatar-stack-overflow.ts:13-24` says display + edit must share deterministic formula | Ref never attaches, so PeoplePicker never computes formula override. Same 180px width then falls back to Combobox DOM `useOverflowCount`, reintroducing length-dependent drift. Fix direction: make internal `NativeCombobox` / `CustomCombobox` forward refs and pass public `ref` to the actual trigger/root DOM, without changing Combobox API. |
| Select open searchable selected-label overlay applies `truncate` to flex container instead of real text box | `select.tsx:196-215`; W3C CSS Overflow `text-overflow`; Mozilla Bug 972664 comment 1; `person-display.tsx:142-150` existing DS fix uses outer flex + inner `truncate flex-1 min-w-0` | Raw text inside `inline-flex` becomes anonymous flex item, so ellipsis is applied to wrong box. Fix direction: keep absolute overlay, but use outer `flex items-center` and inner real `<span className="min-w-0 flex-1 truncate">selectedLabel</span>`. |
| SSOT drift allowed repeat false fixes | `people-picker.spec.md:119-144` requires length=1 and single closed use shared `PersonDisplay` ellipsis; `field-controls.spec.md:286-288` requires shared selected renderer; `people-picker.spec.md:127-134` requires length≥2 avatar stack + round +N | Prior fixes targeted downstream selectors/measurement (`root.matches`, `querySelector`, fallback widths) but no automated assertion proved `stackContainerRef.current !== null` or `visibleCountOverride` is actually consumed. Add regression assertions around ref attachment + visible count for length 3/4 at fixed width, and around overlay `scrollWidth > clientWidth` with visible ellipsis. |

Why prior ships missed it: the visual component still rendered, so ordinary screenshots did not expose the missing ref unless the test asserted the overflow algorithm path. The `_ref` smell was also hidden by intentional `_ref` cases elsewhere.

## DS-Wide Ref-Drop Iceberg

`rg "_ref"` found:

- `Combobox`: **real bug**. Public ref dropped at `combobox.tsx:642-647`.
- `SelectMenu`: intentional composite no DOM host, documented at `select-menu.tsx:119-122`, `_ref` at `select-menu.tsx:148`.
- `DateGrid`: intentional DayPicker no single DOM ref target, documented at `date-grid.tsx:66-67`.
- `Toast/Toaster`: intentional Sonner portal no DOM target, documented at `toast.tsx:91-94`.
- `FileViewer/image-renderer.tsx`: callback param, not React `forwardRef`.

So iceberg is small: **Combobox is the actionable leaked ref-drop pattern**.
